Body

Media type: application/json - Video Example

Type: object

Properties
  • version: required(string)

    {R} Version of the API

  • label: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} UUID resource

  • source_id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} ID of Parent Source

  • type: required(string)

    {R} Type of ASIC platform

  • name: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • network: required(object)

    Network section of a flow

    • src_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Source IP Address

    • src_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Source UPD port

    • dst_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Destination IP Address

    • dst_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Destination UPD port

    • dst_mac: required(string - pattern: \b([0-9a-fA-F]{2}:??){5}([0-9a-fA-F]{2})\b)

      {R/W} Destination MAC address

    • vlan_tag: required(string)

      {R/W} VLAN number, 0 for untagged

    • ssrc: required(string)

      {R/W} SSRC Number

    • enable: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Control of flow:

      • 0 = Disabled
      • 1 = Enabled
    • pkt_cnt: required(string)

      {R} Packet counter

    • rtp_pt: required(string)

      {R/W} RTP Payload type

    • ttl: required(string)

      {R/W} IP TTL

    • dscp: required(string)

      {R/W} IP DSCP

  • format: required(object)

    Video format

    • format_type: required(one of video, audio, ancillary)

      {R} Format type

    • sdp_file_url: required(string)

      {R} Url of the SDP file describing the flow

    • format_code_valid: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R} Video Format validity flag

      • 0 = invalid
      • 1 = valid
    • format_code_t_scan: required(one of 0, 4)

      {R} Transport scan

      • 0 = interlace
      • 4 = progressive
    • format_code_p_scan: required(one of 0, 4)

      {R} Picture scan

      • 0 = interlace
      • 4 = progressive
    • format_code_mode: required(one of 0, 8, 16, 32, 40)

      {R} Format

      • 0 = HD
      • 8 = SD
      • 16 = 3G
      • 32 = 6G
      • 40 = 12G
    • format_code_format: required(one of 0, 2, 64, 512, 576)

      {R} Video Format

      • 0 = 1920x1080 or 3840x2160 if format code mode is 6G or 12G
      • 2 = 2048x1080 or 4096x2160 if format code mode is 6G or 12G
      • 64 = 1270x720
      • 512 = 525i
      • 576 = 625i
    • format_code_rate: required(one of 2040, 3072, 5120, 6144, 7168, 9216, 10240, 11264)

      {R} Video rate

      • 255 = invalid
      • 2040 = 29.98hz
      • 3072 = 24hz
      • 5120 = 25hz or 50hz for 1080i
      • 6144 = 29.97hz or 59.94hz for 1080i
      • 7168 = 30hz or 60hz for 1080i
      • 9216 = 50hz
      • 10240 = 59.94hz
      • 11264 = 60hz
    • format_rx_code_rate: required(one of 2040, 3072, 5120, 6144, 7168, 9216, 10240, 11264)

      {R} Video rate received.

      • 255 = invalid
      • 2040 = 29.98hz
      • 3072 = 24hz
      • 5120 = 25hz or 50hz for 1080i
      • 6144 = 29.97hz or 59.94hz for 1080i
      • 7168 = 30hz or 60hz for 1080i
      • 9216 = 50hz
      • 10240 = 59.94hz
      • 11264 = 60hz
    • format_code_sampling: required(one of 0, 8192)

      {R} Video sampling

      • 0 = interlace
      • 8192 = progressive
    • format_bit_depth: required(one of 10, 12)

      {R} Video bit depth.

    • format_colorimetry: required(one of BT709, BT2020)

      {R} Video colorimetry.

    • format_tcs: required(one of SDR, HLG, PQ)

      {R} Video transfer characteristic

    • format_ictcp: required(one of true, false)

      {R} Video ICtCp active.

  • jumbo_frame: required(one of 0, 1)

    {R/W} Allows to send one entire video line in a IP RTP frame.

    • 0 = Disabled
    • 1 = Enabled

Example:

{
  "version": "2",
  "label": "st2110 flow",
  "id": "a04f66a2-9910-11e5-8894-feff819cdc9f",
  "source_id": "a0008e96-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
  "type": "3",
  "name": "1_0",
  "network": {
    "src_ip_addr": "192.168.39.221",
    "src_udp_port": "10000",
    "dst_ip_addr": "239.22.1.1",
    "dst_udp_port": "20000",
    "dst_mac": "01:00:5e:16:01:01",
    "vlan_tag": "0",
    "ssrc": "0",
    "pkt_cnt": "42787548",
    "rtp_pt": "96",
    "ttl": "64",
    "dscp": "0",
    "enable": "1"
  },
  "format": {
    "format_type": "video",
    "sdp_file_url": "192.168.39.221/emsfp/node/v1/sdp/a04f66a2-9910-11e5-8894-feff819cdc9f",
    "format_code_valid": "1",
    "format_code_t_scan": "0",
    "format_code_p_scan": "0",
    "format_code_mode": "0",
    "format_code_format": "0",
    "format_code_rate": "6144",
    "format_code_sampling": "0",
    "format_rx_code_rate": "6144",
    "format_bit_depth": 10,
    "format_colorimetry": "BT709",
    "format_tcs": "SDR",
    "format_ictcp": false
  },
  "jumbo_frame": "0"
}

Media type: application/json - Audio Example

Type: object

Properties
  • version: required(string)

    {R} Version of the API

  • label: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} UUID resource

  • source_id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} ID of Parent Source

  • type: required(string)

    {R} Type of ASIC platform

  • name: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • network: required(object)

    Network section of a flow

    • src_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Source IP Address

    • src_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Source UPD port

    • dst_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Destination IP Address

    • dst_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Destination UPD port

    • dst_mac: required(string - pattern: \b([0-9a-fA-F]{2}:??){5}([0-9a-fA-F]{2})\b)

      {R/W} Destination MAC address

    • vlan_tag: required(string)

      {R/W} VLAN number, 0 for untagged

    • ssrc: required(string)

      {R/W} SSRC Number

    • enable: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Control of flow:

      • 0 = Disabled
      • 1 = Enabled
    • pkt_cnt: required(string)

      {R} Packet counter

    • rtp_pt: required(string)

      {R/W} RTP Payload type

    • ttl: required(string)

      {R/W} IP TTL

    • dscp: required(string)

      {R/W} IP DSCP

  • format: required(object)

    Audio Format information

    • format_type: required(one of video, audio, ancillary)

      {R} Format type

    • sdp_file_url: required(string)

      {R} Url of the SDP file describing the flow

    • format_code_rate: required(one of 0, 48000)

      {R} Audio sample rate in Hz (ex: 48000 -> 48kHz)

    • aud_chan_map: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{4}$)

      {R/W} Considering a 16 bits representation of the aud_chan_map parameter, set to one the corresponding bit to enable the embedding of the respective audio channel within the RTP flow.

      • bit 0 -> emdev SDI audio channel 0
      • bit 1 -> emdev SDI audio channel 1
      • bit 2 -> emdev SDI audio channel 2
      • ...
      • bit 15 -> emdev SDI audio channel 15

      The resulting 16 bit vector value is then configured in its MSB first hexadecimal representation. For example, if you want to map channels 0,1,5 and 15 to the flow, the aud_chan_map value should be "8023".

      NOTE Refer to the UserGuide for more details on Audio Channel mapping.

    • aud_ptime_idx: required(one of 0, 1, 2, 3, 5)

      {R/W} AES67 audio packet time can be configured using the aud_ptime_idx field.

      • 0 = 1ms
      • 1 = 125us
      • 2 = 250us
      • 3 = 333us
      • 5 = 500us
    • aud_format: required(one of dash-30, dash-31)

      {R/W} AES67 Audio format (Uncompressed, Compressed).

Example:

{
  "version": "2",
  "label": "st2110 flow",
  "id": "a14f66a2-9910-11e5-8894-feff819cdc9f",
  "source_id": "a0018e96-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
  "type": "3",
  "name": "100_0",
  "network": {
    "src_ip_addr": "192.168.39.36",
    "src_udp_port": "10000",
    "dst_ip_addr": "239.32.100.1",
    "dst_udp_port": "20000",
    "dst_mac": "01:00:5e:20:64:01",

    "dscp": "0",
    "enable": "1"

    "format_code_rate": "48000",
    "aud_chan_map": "0003",

Media type: application/json - Ancillary Example

Type: object

Properties
  • version: required(string)

    {R} Version of the API

  • label: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

  • id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} UUID resource

  • source_id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} ID of Parent Source

  • type: required(string)

    {R} Type of ASIC platform

  • name: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • network: required(object)

    Network section of a flow

    • src_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Source IP Address

    • src_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Source UPD port

    • dst_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Destination IP Address

    • dst_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Destination UPD port

    • dst_mac: required(string - pattern: \b([0-9a-fA-F]{2}:??){5}([0-9a-fA-F]{2})\b)

      {R/W} Destination MAC address

    • vlan_tag: required(string)

      {R/W} VLAN number, 0 for untagged

    • ssrc: required(string)

      {R/W} SSRC Number

    • enable: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Control of flow:

      • 0 = Disabled
      • 1 = Enabled
    • pkt_cnt: required(string)

      {R} Packet counter

    • rtp_pt: required(string)

      {R/W} RTP Payload type

    • ttl: required(string)

      {R/W} IP TTL

    • dscp: required(string)

      {R/W} IP DSCP

  • format: required(object)

    Audio Format information

    • format_type: required(one of video, audio, ancillary)

      {R} Format type

    • sdp_file_url: required(string)

      {R} Url of the SDP file describing the flow

    • anc_flow_profile: required(one of 0, 1, 2)

      {R/W} Ancillary flow profile.

      • 0 = 2110-40 RTP packet is transmitted only when full or on end of frame/end-of-field event.
      • 1 = 2110-40 RTP packet is forced to be sent after a 1ms timeout fromd ecoding of ancillary packet inside the SDI stream.
      • 2 = 2110-40 RTP packet is transmitted every single ancillary packet (all ancillary packets decoded from the SDI stream are send individually over RTP).

Media type: application/json - Video Example

Properties
  • label: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • name: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • network: required(object)

    Network section of a flow

    • src_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Source IP Address

    • src_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Source UPD port

    • dst_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Destination IP Address

    • dst_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Destination UPD port

    • dst_mac: required(string - pattern: \b([0-9a-fA-F]{2}:??){5}([0-9a-fA-F]{2})\b)

      {R/W} Destination MAC address

    • vlan_tag: required(string)

      {R/W} VLAN number, 0 for untagged

    • ssrc: required(string)

      {R/W} SSRC Number

    • enable: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Control of flow:

      • 0 = Disabled
      • 1 = Enabled
    • rtp_pt: required(string)

      {R/W} RTP Payload type

    • ttl: required(string)

      {R/W} IP TTL

    • dscp: required(string)

      {R/W} IP DSCP

  • jumbo_frame: required(one of 0, 1)

    {R/W} Allows to send one entire video line in a IP RTP frame.

    • 0 = Disabled
    • 1 = Enabled

Example:

{
  "label": "st2110 flow",
  "name": "1_0",
  "network": {
    "src_ip_addr": "192.168.39.221",
    "src_udp_port": "10000",
    "dst_ip_addr": "239.22.1.1",
    "dst_udp_port": "20000",
    "dst_mac": "01:00:5e:16:01:01",
    "vlan_tag": "0",
    "ssrc": "0",
    "rtp_pt": "96",
    "ttl": "64",
    "dscp": "0",
    "enable": "1"
  },
  "jumbo_frame": "0"
}

Media type: application/json - Audio Example

Type: object

Properties
  • label: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • name: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • network: required(object)

    Network section of a flow

    • src_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Source IP Address

    • src_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Source UPD port

    • dst_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Destination IP Address

    • dst_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Destination UPD port

    • dst_mac: required(string - pattern: \b([0-9a-fA-F]{2}:??){5}([0-9a-fA-F]{2})\b)

      {R/W} Destination MAC address

    • vlan_tag: required(string)

      {R/W} VLAN number, 0 for untagged

    • ssrc: required(string)

      {R/W} SSRC Number

    • enable: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Control of flow:

      • 0 = Disabled
      • 1 = Enabled
    • rtp_pt: required(string)

      {R/W} RTP Payload type

    • ttl: required(string)

      {R/W} IP TTL

    • dscp: required(string)

      {R/W} IP DSCP

  • format: required(object)

    Audio Format information

    • aud_chan_map: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{4}$)

      {R/W} Considering a 16 bits representation of the aud_chan_map parameter, set to one the corresponding bit to enable the embedding of the respective audio channel within the RTP flow.

      • bit 0 -> emdev SDI audio channel 0
      • bit 1 -> emdev SDI audio channel 1
      • bit 2 -> emdev SDI audio channel 2
      • ...
      • bit 15 -> emdev SDI audio channel 15

      The resulting 16 bit vector value is then configured in its MSB first hexadecimal representation. For example, if you want to map channels 0,1,5 and 15 to the flow, the aud_chan_map value should be "8023".

      NOTE Refer to the UserGuide for more details on Audio Channel mapping.

    • aud_ptime_idx: required(one of 0, 1, 2, 3, 5)

      {R/W} AES67 audio packet time can be configured using the aud_ptime_idx field.

      • 0 = 1ms
      • 1 = 125us
      • 2 = 250us
      • 3 = 333us
      • 5 = 500us
    • aud_format: required(one of dash-30, dash-31)

      {R/W} AES67 Audio format (Uncompressed, Compressed).

Example:

{
  "label": "st2110 flow",
  "name": "100_0",
  "network": {
    "src_ip_addr": "192.168.39.36",
    "src_udp_port": "10000",
    "dst_ip_addr": "239.32.100.1",
    "dst_udp_port": "20000",
    "dst_mac": "01:00:5e:20:64:01",
    "vlan_tag": "0",
    "ssrc": "0",
    "rtp_pt": "97",
    "ttl": "64",
    "dscp": "0",
    "enable": "1"
  },
  "format": {
    "aud_chan_map": "0003",
    "aud_ptime_idx": "5",
    "aud_format": "dash-31"
  }
}

Media type: application/json - Ancillary Example

Type: object

Properties
  • label: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • name: required(string - minLength: 1 - maxLength: 16)

    {R/W} Free form string label for one of the resource

  • network: required(object)

    Network section of a flow

    • src_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Source IP Address

    • src_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Source UPD port

    • dst_ip_addr: required(string - pattern: ^(?:[0-9]{1,3}\.){3}[0-9]{1,3}$)

      {R/W} Destination IP Address

    • dst_udp_port: required(string - pattern: ^(6553[0-5]|655[0-2]\d|65[0-4]\d\d|6[0-4]\d{3}|[1-5]\d{4}|[1-9]\d{0,3}|0)$)

      {R/W} Destination UPD port

    • dst_mac: required(string - pattern: \b([0-9a-fA-F]{2}:??){5}([0-9a-fA-F]{2})\b)

      {R/W} Destination MAC address

    • vlan_tag: required(string)

      {R/W} VLAN number, 0 for untagged

    • ssrc: required(string)

      {R/W} SSRC Number

    • enable: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Control of flow:

      • 0 = Disabled
      • 1 = Enabled
    • rtp_pt: required(string)

      {R/W} RTP Payload type

    • ttl: required(string)

      {R/W} IP TTL

    • dscp: required(string)

      {R/W} IP DSCP

  • format: required(object)

    Audio Format information

    • anc_flow_profile: required(one of 0, 1, 2)

      {R/W} Ancillary flow profile.

      • 0 = 2110-40 RTP packet is transmitted only when full or on end of frame/end-of-field event.
      • 1 = 2110-40 RTP packet is forced to be sent after a 1ms timeout fromd ecoding of ancillary packet inside the SDI stream.
      • 2 = 2110-40 RTP packet is transmitted every single ancillary packet (all ancillary packets decoded from the SDI stream are send individually over RTP).

Example:

{
  "label": "st2110 flow",
  "name": "100_0",
  "network": {
    "src_ip_addr": "192.168.39.36",
    "src_udp_port": "10000",
    "dst_ip_addr": "239.42.100.1",
    "dst_udp_port": "20000",
    "dst_mac": "01:00:5e:2a:64:01",
    "vlan_tag": "0",
    "ssrc": "0",
    "rtp_pt": "100",
    "ttl": "64",
    "dscp": "0",
    "enable": "1"
  },
  "format": {
    "anc_flow_profile": "2"
  }
}

/clean_switch

/clean_switch get

get

Get Clean Switch engine identifier list.

get /clean_switch

Get Clean Switch engine identifier list.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: any

Example:

[
  "a0e61a30-990b-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f/",
  "b0e61a30-990b-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f/"
]

/clean_switch/{cleanSwitchId} get put

get

Get Clean Switch configuration.

put

Changes Clean switch_time configurations.

get /clean_switch/{cleanSwitchId}

Get Clean Switch configuration.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • cleanSwitchId: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    Valid Clean Switch engine identifier.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/sdp

Type: object

Properties
  • clean_switch: required(object)

    Clean Switch related configuration.

    • mode: required(one of disabled, enabled, video_only)

      {R/W} Clean switch mode.

      • disabled: No clean switch is performed.
      • enabled: Clean switch will occurs when switch_time is set to 'now'
      • video_only: Clean switch will only affect video, and will be triggered by switch_time set to 'now', OR, when a combined SDP (primary and secondary) is set by the API.
    • switch_time: required(one of idle, now)

      {R/W} Switch time specified time. Currently only supporting "now". Therefore, the user can preconfigure the flows, and select when the switching occurs.

    • igmp_setup_delay: required(string)

      {R/W} The IGMP setup delay is used to specify the time the global setup will take to route the new traffic once the clean switch is performed. A value too small will create missing frame on the switched flows, and a value too big will "disabled" the (-7) option for a longer period. This value is in milliseconds.

      NOTE A delay of '0' will result in a infinite timeout (packet needs to be received in order to switch. Delay of 0, can only be used when timeout_option is NOT revert and type is 'mbb'.

    • type: required(one of bbm, mbb)

      {R/W} Select the type of clean switch you prefer.

      • "bbm": Break before make. Uses less bandwidth, but may freeze during switch for a second.
      • "mbb": Make before break. Guarantees a clean transition at the cost of more bandwidth during the switch.
    • timeout_option: required(string)

      {R/W} Select the timeout option to apply. If the igmp_setup_delay timer elapsed, what action should we take.

      • "switch": Perform switch anyway.
      • "revert": Remain on the actual flows, will change the flows configuration to reflect revert. (can only be used when "igmp_setup_delay" != 0)

      NOTE Only available when "type" is "mbb".

    • status: required(string)

      {R} Current clean switch status.

      • "ok": Idle mode, or last activation successful.
      • "pending": A clean switch is pending (need to set the switch_time).
      • "in_progress": A clean switch is being processed.
      • "failed": Last clean switch failed (refer to timeout option for action taken by device).

Example:

{
  "clean_switch": {
    "mode": "disabled",
    "switch_time": "idle",
    "igmp_setup_delay": "300",
    "type": "bbm",
    "timeout_option": "switch",
    "status": "ok"
  }
}

HTTP status code 400

Invalid Clean Switch identifier

Body

Media type: application/sdp

Type: any

put /clean_switch/{cleanSwitchId}

Changes Clean switch_time configurations.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • cleanSwitchId: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    Valid Clean Switch engine identifier.

Body

Media type: application/sdp

Type: object

Properties
  • clean_switch: required(object)

    Clean Switch related configuration.

    • mode: required(one of disabled, enabled, video_only)

      {R/W} Clean switch mode.

      • disabled: No clean switch is performed.
      • enabled: Clean switch will occurs when switch_time is set to 'now'
      • video_only: Clean switch will only affect video, and will be triggered by switch_time set to 'now', OR, when a combined SDP (primary and secondary) is set by the API.
    • switch_time: required(one of idle, now)

      {R/W} Switch time specified time. Currently only supporting "now". Therefore, the user can preconfigure the flows, and select when the switching occurs.

    • igmp_setup_delay: required(string)

      {R/W} The IGMP setup delay is used to specify the time the global setup will take to route the new traffic once the clean switch is performed. A value too small will create missing frame on the switched flows, and a value too big will "disabled" the (-7) option for a longer period. This value is in milliseconds.

      NOTE A delay of '0' will result in a infinite timeout (packet needs to be received in order to switch. Delay of 0, can only be used when timeout_option is NOT revert and type is 'mbb'.

    • type: required(one of bbm, mbb)

      {R/W} Select the type of clean switch you prefer.

      • "bbm": Break before make. Uses less bandwidth, but may freeze during switch for a second.
      • "mbb": Make before break. Guarantees a clean transition at the cost of more bandwidth during the switch.
    • timeout_option: required(string)

      {R/W} Select the timeout option to apply. If the igmp_setup_delay timer elapsed, what action should we take.

      • "switch": Perform switch anyway.
      • "revert": Remain on the actual flows, will change the flows configuration to reflect revert. (can only be used when "igmp_setup_delay" != 0)

      NOTE Only available when "type" is "mbb".

Example:

{
  "clean_switch": {
    "mode": "enabled",
    "switch_time": "now",
    "igmp_setup_delay": "300",
    "type": "mbb",
    "timeout_option": "revert"
  }
}

/sdi

/sdi get put

get

Display the current sdi operating bit rate.

put

Changes the current sdi operating bit rate.

get /sdi

Display the current sdi operating bit rate.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • operating_bit_rate: required(one of integer, fractional)

    {R/W} Currently selected bitrate is either integer (x/1) or fractional (x/1.001).

    • "integer" - Bit rate is integer, for example: 30 hz, 60 hz, etc.
    • "fractional" - Bit rate is fractional, for example: 29.97 hz, 59.94 hz, etc.

Example:

{
  "configuration": {
    "operating_bit_rate": "fractional"
  }
}

put /sdi

Changes the current sdi operating bit rate.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • operating_bit_rate: required(one of integer, fractional)

    {R/W} Currently selected bitrate is either integer (x/1) or fractional (x/1.001).

    • "integer" - Bit rate is integer, for example: 30 hz, 60 hz, etc.
    • "fractional" - Bit rate is fractional, for example: 29.97 hz, 59.94 hz, etc.

Example:

{
  "configuration": {
    "operating_bit_rate": "fractional"
  }
}

/port/{portId} get put

get

Get a particular port's information.

put

Change the specified port's caracteristics.

get /port/{portId}

Get a particular port's information.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • portId: (integer)

    Valid Port identifier.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json - non management port

Type: object

Properties
  • link: required(one of up, down)

    {R} Link state description.

  • capabilities: required(one of 10Gbps, 25Gbps)

    {R} Speed capabilities of this port.

  • speed: required(one of 10Gbps, 25Gbps)

    {R} Current interface speed.

  • sfp_type_capabilities: required(one of "msa, n-msa", n-msa, msa)

    {R} Supported sfp types by this port. Only one type at a time.

  • sfp_type: required(one of msa, n-msa, auto)

    Hardware SFP auto-detect option installed:

    • {R} This field always indicates "auto" and can't be modified.

    Hardware SFP auto-detect option not installed:

    • {R/W} Indicates the currently selected sfp type by this port. This active type has to be listed in the sfp type capabilities string and cannot be "auto".
  • detected_sfp_type: required(one of msa, n-msa, invalid, N/A)

    {R} Currently detected SFP type when "sfp_type" is configured in "auto" mode. Otherwise, this field is set to "N/A".

  • host_pinout: required(one of 2R, 2T, RT, BB)

    {R/W} Currently selected sfp host pinout type by this port. If modified, the flows associated with this port will lose their configuration and the device will reboot.

    • 2R: Two SDI inputs.
    • 2T: Two SDI outputs.
    • RT: One SDI input and one SDI output.
    • BB: Black burst synchronization output.

Example:

{
  "link": "up",
  "capabilities": "25Gbps, 10Gbps",
  "speed": "25Gbps",
  "sfp_type_capabilities": "msa, n-msa",
  "sfp_type": "auto",
  "detected_sfp_type": "n-msa",
  "host_pinout": "2R"
}

Media type: application/json - management port

Type: object

Properties
  • link: required(one of up, down)

    {R} Link state description.

  • capabilities: required(one of 10Gbps, 25Gbps)

    {R} Speed capabilities of this port.

  • speed: required(one of 10Gbps, 25Gbps)

    {R} Current interface speed.

  • sfp_type_capabilities: required(one of "msa, n-msa", n-msa, msa)

    {R} Supported sfp types by this port. Only one type at a time.

  • sfp_type: required(one of msa, n-msa, auto)

    Hardware SFP auto-detect option installed:

    • {R} This field always indicates "auto" and can't be modified.

    Hardware SFP auto-detect option not installed:

    • {R/W} Indicates the currently selected sfp type by this port. This active type has to be listed in the sfp type capabilities string and cannot be "auto".
  • detected_sfp_type: required(one of msa, n-msa, invalid, N/A)

    {R} Currently detected SFP type when "sfp_type" is configured in "auto" mode. Otherwise, this field is set to "N/A".

  • host_pinout: required(one of 2R, 2T, RT, BB)

    {R/W} Currently selected sfp host pinout type by this port. If modified, the flows associated with this port will lose their configuration and the device will reboot.

    • 2R: Two SDI inputs.
    • 2T: Two SDI outputs.
    • RT: One SDI input and one SDI output.
    • BB: Black burst synchronization output.
  • sfp_ddm_info: required(object)

    SFP DDM Diagnostics information.

    • temperature: required(object)

      Temperature diagnostics information in Celsius.

      • high_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High alarm threshold.

      • low_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low alarm threshold.

      • high_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High warning threshold.

      • low_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low warning threshold.

      • current: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Current value.

    • vcc: required(object)

      VCC diagnostics information in mV.

      • high_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High alarm threshold.

      • low_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low alarm threshold.

      • high_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High warning threshold.

      • low_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low warning threshold.

      • current: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Current value.

    • tx_bias: required(object)

      TX BIAS diagnostics information in uA.

      • high_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High alarm threshold.

      • low_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low alarm threshold.

      • high_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High warning threshold.

      • low_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low warning threshold.

      • current: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Current value.

    • tx_power: required(object)

      TX Power diagnostics information in uW.

      • high_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High alarm threshold.

      • low_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low alarm threshold.

      • high_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High warning threshold.

      • low_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low warning threshold.

      • current: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Current value.

    • rx_power: required(object)

      RX Power diagnostics information in uW.

      • high_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High alarm threshold.

      • low_alarm: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low alarm threshold.

      • high_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} High warning threshold.

      • low_warning: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Low warning threshold.

      • current: required(union of integer or nil)

        {R} Current value.

    • alarm_status: required(object)

      DDM Alarm status.

      • high_temperature: required(boolean)

        {R} High Temperature reached.

      • low_temperature: required(boolean)

        {R} Low Temperature reached.

      • high_vcc: required(boolean)

        {R} High VCC reached.

      • low_vcc: required(boolean)

        {R} Low VCC reached.

      • high_tx_bias: required(boolean)

        {R} High TX BIAS reached.

      • low_tx_bias: required(boolean)

        {R} Low TX BIAS reached.

      • high_tx_power: required(boolean)

        {R} High TX Power reached.

      • low_tx_power: required(boolean)

        {R} Low TX Power reached.

      • high_rx_power: required(boolean)

        {R} High RX Power reached.

      • low_rx_power: required(boolean)

        {R} Low RX Power reached.

    • warning_status: required(object)

      DDM Warning status.

      • high_temperature: required(boolean)

        {R} High Temperature reached.

      • low_temperature: required(boolean)

        {R} Low Temperature reached.

      • high_vcc: required(boolean)

        {R} High VCC reached.

      • low_vcc: required(boolean)

        {R} Low VCC reached.

      • high_tx_bias: required(boolean)

        {R} High TX BIAS reached.

      • low_tx_bias: required(boolean)

        {R} Low TX BIAS reached.

      • high_tx_power: required(boolean)

        {R} High TX Power reached.

      • low_tx_power: required(boolean)

        {R} Low TX Power reached.

      • high_rx_power: required(boolean)

        {R} High RX Power reached.

      • low_rx_power: required(boolean)

        {R} Low RX Power reached.

Example:

{
  "link": "up",
  "capabilities": "25Gbps, 10Gbps",
  "speed": "25Gbps",
  "sfp_type_capabilities": "msa",
  "sfp_type": "msa",
  "detected_sfp_type": "N/A",
  "host_pinout": "RT",
  "sfp_ddm_info": {
    "temperature": {
      "high_alarm": 85.00,
      "low_alarm": -15.00,
      "high_warning": 80.00,
      "low_warning": -10.00,
      "current": 33.988
    },
    "vcc": {
      "high_alarm": 3.500,
      "low_alarm": 3.100,
      "high_warning": 3.470,

HTTP status code 400

Invalid port identifier.

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: any

put /port/{portId}

Change the specified port's caracteristics.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • portId: (integer)

    Valid Port identifier.

Body

Media type: application/json - multiple fields

Type: object

Properties
  • sfp_type: (one of msa, n-msa, auto)

    Hardware SFP auto-detect option installed:

    • {R} This field always indicates "auto" and can't be modified.

    Hardware SFP auto-detect option not installed:

    • {R/W} Indicates the currently selected sfp type by this port. This active type has to be listed in the sfp type capabilities string and cannot be "auto".
  • host_pinout: required(one of 2R, 2T, RT, BB)

    {R/W} Currently selected sfp host pinout type by this port. If modified, the flows associated with this port will lose their configuration and the device will reboot.

    • 2R: Two SDI inputs.
    • 2T: Two SDI outputs.
    • RT: One SDI input and one SDI output.
    • BB: Black burst synchronization output.

Example:

{
  "sfp_type": "n-msa",
  "host_pinout": "2R"
}

Media type: application/json - single field

Type: object

Properties
  • sfp_type: (one of msa, n-msa, auto)

    Hardware SFP auto-detect option installed:

    • {R} This field always indicates "auto" and can't be modified.

    Hardware SFP auto-detect option not installed:

    • {R/W} Indicates the currently selected sfp type by this port. This active type has to be listed in the sfp type capabilities string and cannot be "auto".
  • host_pinout: required(one of 2R, 2T, RT, BB)

    {R/W} Currently selected sfp host pinout type by this port. If modified, the flows associated with this port will lose their configuration and the device will reboot.

    • 2R: Two SDI inputs.
    • 2T: Two SDI outputs.
    • RT: One SDI input and one SDI output.
    • BB: Black burst synchronization output.

Example:

{
  "host_pinout": "2R"
}

/route/bulk/receiver/{uuid} put

put

Set the routing parameters for a specific device.

put /route/bulk/receiver/{uuid}

Set the routing parameters for a specific device.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • uuid: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    Valid BULK routing receiver identifier.

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: array of object

Items: bulkRouteObject

  • id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {W} UUID resource

  • params: required(object)
    • sdp: required(string)

      {W} SDP File string (with textual \r\n for end-of-line).

Example:

[
  {
    "id": "3000000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "params": {
      "sdp": "v=0\r\no=- 1443716955 1443716955 IN IP4 192.168.4.111\r\ns=Box6_Sebas 0-0-0\r\nt=0 0\r\na=group:DUP primary secondary\r\nm=video 20000 RTP/AVP 96\r\nc=IN IP4 239.20.212.1/64\r\na=source-filter: incl IN IP4 239.20.212.1 192.168.2.212\r\na=rtpmap:96 raw/90000\r\na=fmtp:96 sampling=YCbCr-4:2:2; width=1920; height=1080; exactframerate=30000/1001; depth=10; TCS=SDR; colorimetry=BT709; PM=2110GPM; SSN=ST2110-20:2017; TP=2110TPN; interlace;\r\na=mediaclk:direct=0\r\na=ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE1588-2008:08-00-11-ff-fe-22-91-bb:0\r\na=mid:primary\r\nm=video 20000 RTP/AVP 96\r\nc=IN IP4 239.120.212.1/64\r\na=source-filter: incl IN IP4 239.120.212.1 192.168.2.212\r\na=rtpmap:96 raw/90000\r\na=fmtp:96 sampling=YCbCr-4:2:2; width=1920; height=1080; exactframerate=30000/1001; depth=10; TCS=SDR; colorimetry=BT709; PM=2110GPM; SSN=ST2110-20:2017; TP=2110TPN; interlace;\r\na=mediaclk:direct=0\r\na=ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE1588-2008:08-00-11-ff-fe-22-91-bb:0\r\na=mid:secondary\r\n"
    }
  },
  {
    "id":"3001000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "params":{
      "sdp":"v=0\r\no=- 1443716955 1443716955 IN IP4 192.168.4.111\r\ns=Box6_Sebas 0-1-0\r\nt=0 0\r\na=group:DUP primary secondary\r\nm=audio 20000 RTP/AVP 97\r\nc=IN IP4 239.30.212.5/64\r\na=source-filter: incl IN IP4 239.30.212.5 192.168.2.212\r\na=rtpmap:97 L24/48000/16\r\na=mediaclk:direct=0 rate=48000\r\na=framecount:6\r\na=ptime:0.125\r\na=ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE1588-2008:08-00-11-ff-fe-22-91-bb:0\r\na=mid:primary\r\nm=audio 20000 RTP/AVP 97\r\nc=IN IP4 239.130.212.5/64\r\na=source-filter: incl IN IP4 239.130.212.5 192.168.2.212\r\na=rtpmap:97 L24/48000/16\r\na=mediaclk:direct=0 rate=48000\r\na=framecount:6\r\na=ptime:0.125\r\na=ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE1588-2008:08-00-11-ff-fe-22-91-bb:0\r\na=mid:secondary\r\n"
    }
  },
  {

HTTP status code 200

A JSON indicating the results for each object in PUT array.

Body

Media type: application/json - success

Type: array of object

Items: bulkRouteResponseObject

  • id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} UUID resource

  • code: required(integer)

    Validation code (based on HTML error code).

    • 200 -> Configuration accepted.
    • 400 -> Error in configuration.
      • on a 400 other field will be available:

Example:

[
  {
    "id": "3000000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  },
  {
    "id": "3001000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  },
  {
    "id": "3002000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  },
  {
    "id": "3003000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  },
  {
    "id": "3004000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  },
  {
    "id": "3005000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  }
]

Media type: application/json - some failure

Type: array of object

Items: bulkRouteResponseFailedObject

  • id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} UUID resource

  • code: required(integer)

    Validation code (based on HTML error code).

    • 200 -> Configuration accepted.
    • 400 -> Error in configuration.
  • error: required(string)

    Text message giving information on failure.

  • debug: required(string)

Example:

[
  {
    "id": "3000000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  },
  {
    "id": "300100sd0a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9",
    "code": 400,
    "error": "Invalid UUID",
    "debug": null
  },
  {
    "id": "3002000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 400,
    "error": "Invalid parameter",
    "debug": null
  },
  {
    "id": "3003000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  },
  {
    "id": "3004000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  },
  {
    "id": "3005000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
    "code": 200
  }
]

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • uuid: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    Valid BULK routing sender identifier.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json - success

Type: array of object

Items: bulkRouteReadObject

  • id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} UUID resource

    • sdp: required(string)

/telemetry

/telemetry get

get

Get Telemetry data options.

get /telemetry

Get Telemetry data options.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: any

Example:

[
  "node/",
  "ports/",
  "devices/"
]

/telemetry/node get

get

Get Telemetry NODE data options.

get /telemetry/node

Get Telemetry NODE data options.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • health: required(object)
    • core_temp: required(integer)

      {R} Internal core temperature in Celsius.

    • fan_speed: required(integer)

      {R} Current fan speed in rpm.

    • core_voltage: required(integer)
  • refclk: required(object)
    • status: required(one of 0, 1, 3 - pattern: ^[0-3]$)

      {R} PTP engine status in 8 bits hex value.

      • 0 = PTP not locked
      • 1 = PTP stage 1 lock (coarse lock)
      • 3 = PTP stage 2 lock (locked)
    • grandmaster_id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{2}-[0-9a-f]{2}-[0-9a-f]{2}-[0-9a-f]{2}-[0-9a-f]{2}-[0-9a-f]{2}-[0-9a-f]{2}-[0-9a-f]{2}$)

      {R} Clock identifier.

    • offset_from_master: required(integer)

      {R} Current value of the time difference between our slave engine and the master Reference Clock: 'offsetFromMaster' = 'Time on the slave clock' ─ 'Time on the master clock' in uSec.

    • mean_delay: required(integer)

      {R} Current value of the mean propagation time between the Reference Clock master and our slave clock in uSec.

Example:

{
  "health": {
    "core_temp": 49,
    "fan_speed": 4210,
    "core_voltage": 700
  },
  "refclk": {
    "status": "locked",
    "grandmaster_id": "08-00-11-ff-fe-22-91-bb",
    "offset_from_master": 30,
    "mean_delay": 220
  }
}

/telemetry/ports get

get

Get Telemetry PORTS data options.

get /telemetry/ports

Get Telemetry PORTS data options.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • ports: required(array of TelemetryType.MngtPortType)

    Items: MngtPortType

    • port: required(integer)

      {R} Port identifier.

    • temperature: required(integer)

      {R} SFP temperature in Celsius.

    • vcc: required(integer)

      {R} Input voltage read by SFP in Volt.

    • tx_power: required(integer)

      {R} SFP TX power in uWatt.

    • rx_power: required(integer)

      {R} SFP RX power in uWatt.

Example:

{
  "ports": [
    {
      "port": 3,
      "temperature": 39.500,
      "tx_power": 458,
      "rx_power": 878
    },
    {
      "port": 5,
      "temperature": 0.00,
      "tx_power": 0,
      "rx_power": 0
    }
  ]
}

/telemetry/devices get

get

Get Telemetry DEVICES data options.

get /telemetry/devices

Get Telemetry DEVICES data options.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • devices: required(array of TelemetryType.DevicesDefType)

    Items: DevicesDefType

    • device: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

      {R} Device UUID.

    • type: required(one of encapsulator, decapsultor)

      {R} Device type (encapsulator, decapsulator)

    • flow_to_ptp_offset: required(object)

      {R} Flow to PTP offset information. Only available for 'decapsulator' devices.

      • primary: required(integer)

        Primary flow alignment point time difference with PTP (in ns).

      • secondary: required(integer)

        Secondary flow alignment point time difference with PTP (in ns).

    • sdi_to_ptp_offset: required(integer)

      {R} SDI Alignment point to PTP offset in (ns). only available for 'encapsulator' devices.

    • engines: required(array of TelemetryType.EngineObjectType)

      Items: EngineObjectType

      • engine: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

        {R} Engine UUID.

      • essence: required(one of video, audio, ancillary)

        {R} Essence type of this engine.

      • flows: required(array of TelemetryType.FlowsObjectType)

        Items: FlowsObjectType

        • flow: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

          {R} Flow UUID.

        • type: required(one of primary, secondary)

          {R} Flow type (primary or secondary)

        • pkt_cnt: required(integer)

          {R} Flow Packet counter.

        • sequence_error: (integer)

          {R} Flow Sequence error counter. Only available for 'decapsulator' devices.

Example:

{
  "devices": [
    {
      "device": "10e61a30-990b-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
      "channel": 1,
      "valid": false,

          "engine": "1002000a-990d-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",

/black_burst (only available when one port is set to BB)

/black_burst get

get

Get Black Burst identifier list.

get /black_burst

Get Black Burst identifier list.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: any

Example:

[
  "40000000-b1ac-8994-11e5-feff819cdc9f/"
]

/black_burst/{blackBurstId} get put

get

Get Black Burst configuration.

put

Changes Black Burst configurations.

get /black_burst/{blackBurstId}

Get Black Burst configuration.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • blackBurstId: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    Valid Black Burst identifier.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • offset_mode: required(integer - maximum: 1)

    {R/W} Line offset mode to use.

    • 0 = micro second offset mode.
    • 1 = line offset mode.
  • usec_offset: required(integer)

    {R/W} uSecond to offset video from PTP when micro second offset mode is selected.

  • v_offset: required(integer)

    {R/W} Vertical line offset when line offset mode is selected.

  • h_offset: required(integer)

    {R/W} Horizontal pixel offset when line offset mode is selected.

Example:

{
  "offset_mode": 1,
  "usec_offset": 0,
  "v_offset": 0,
  "h_offset": 0
}

HTTP status code 400

Invalid Black Burst identifier

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: any

put /black_burst/{blackBurstId}

Changes Black Burst configurations.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • blackBurstId: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    Valid Black Burst identifier.

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • offset_mode: required(integer - maximum: 1)

    {R/W} Line offset mode to use.

    • 0 = micro second offset mode.
    • 1 = line offset mode.
  • usec_offset: required(integer)

    {R/W} uSecond to offset video from PTP when micro second offset mode is selected.

  • v_offset: required(integer)

    {R/W} Vertical line offset when line offset mode is selected.

  • h_offset: required(integer)

    {R/W} Horizontal pixel offset when line offset mode is selected.

Example:

{
  "offset_mode": 1,
  "usec_offset": 0,
  "v_offset": 10,
  "h_offset": 20
}

HTTP status code 200

The data PUT'd

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: any

HTTP status code 400

Malformed request

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: any

/sdi_input

/sdi_input get

get

Get SDI input identifier list.

get /sdi_input

Get SDI input identifier list.

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: any

Example:

[
  "b0d2da17-360a-4396-80a9-f620c4bb3885/",
  "b1d2da17-360a-4396-80a9-f620c4bb3885/"
]

/sdi_input/{sdiInputId} get put

get

Get SDI input configuration.

put

Changes SDI input configurations.

get /sdi_input/{sdiInputId}

Get SDI input configuration.

  • Request
  • Response

URI Parameters

  • sdiInputId: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    Valid SDI Input identifier.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/sdp

Type: object

Properties
  • version: required(string)

    {R} API Version.

  • label: required(string - maxLength: 16)

    {R} Label to identify this SDI Input.

  • id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} UUID resource

  • device_id: required(string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    {R} UUID resource

  • line_offset: required(object)

    Line offset configurations.

    • frame_sync: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Frame sync feature.

      • 0 = Disable frame sync feature.
      • 1 = Enable frame sync feature.
    • offset_mode: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Line offset mode to use.

      • 0 = micro second offset mode.
      • 1 = line offset mode.
    • usec_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} uSecond to offset video from PTP when micro second offset mode is selected.

    • v_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} Vertical line offset when line offset mode is selected.

    • h_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} Horizontal pixel offset when line offset mode is selected.

    • video_rate_convert: required(string)

      {R/W} Frame rate converter.

      • auto: Will not perform rate convertion, input rate will be output rate.
      • 24000/1001 = 23.97hz
      • 24 = 24hz
      • 25 = 25hz
      • 30000/1001 = 29.97hz
      • 30 = 30hz
      • 48000/1001 = 47.95hz
      • 48 = 48hz
      • 50 = 50hz
      • 60000/1001 = 59.94hz
      • 60 = 60hz

Example:

{
  "version": "1",
  "label": "SDI 1",
  "id": "b0d2da17-360a-4396-80a9-f620c4bb3885",
  "device_id": "a0e61a30-990b-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
  "line_offset": {
    "frame_sync": "0",
    "offset_mode": "1",
    "usec_offset": "0",
    "v_offset": "0",
    "h_offset": "0",
    "video_rate_convert": "auto"
  }
}

HTTP status code 400

Invalid SDI input identifier

Body

Media type: application/sdp

Type: any

      • 30 = 30hz

      • 48 = 48hz
      • 50 = 50hz
      • 60000/1001 = 59.94hz
      • 60 = 60hz

Example:

  "line_offset": {
    "frame_sync": "1",

/sdi_output get

get

Get SDI output identifier list.

get /sdi_output

Get SDI output identifier list.

  • Response

Media type: application/json

Type: any

/sdi_output/{sdiOutputId} get put

get

Get SDI output configuration.

put

Changes SDI output configurations.

get /sdi_output/{sdiOutputId}

Get SDI output configuration.

  • Request
  • Response

  • sdiOutputId: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

HTTP status code 200

Type: object

    {R} API Version.

      {R/W} Uses to MAP audio IP streams/channel into the SDI Audio channel.

      • NOTE: String is splitted in 3 sections separated by colon (":")
        • IP stream UUID.
        • IP stream channel identifier (0-15).
        • Enable/Disable (1/0).
      • To unmap a SDI channel: " :0:0"
  • line_offset: required(object)

    Line offset configurations.

    • offset_mode: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Line offset mode to use.

      • 0 = micro second offset mode.
      • 1 = line offset mode.
    • usec_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} uSecond to offset video from PTP when micro second offset mode is selected.

    • v_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} Vertical line offset when line offset mode is selected.

    • h_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} Horizontal pixel offset when line offset mode is selected.

    • audio_delay: required(string)

      {R/W} Audio delay to be applied. In step of 1/freq, where freq can be 48000 or 96000 (if supported by platform).

      • NOTE: Setting 0 will set automatic mode.
    • applied_audio_delay: required(string)

      {R} Audio delay applied, can be different than selected one because it is dependent of the format (mininum and maximum) and can be modified if frame sync is enabled. In step of 1/freq, where freq can be 48000 or 96000 (if supported by platform).

    • status: required(string)

      {R} Status is used to notify of any "warning" in the configuration.

      • 0 = No warning

      • 1 = Sender type configuration and line offset is suspicious.

        ex: Wide sender must at least have the line offset higher than the vertical blanking.

      NOTE: Refer to the UserGuide for more details on SDI Output line offset.

    • frame_buffer: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} FrameBuffer enable switch.

      • 0 = FrameBuffer disabled, precise timing mode.
      • 1 = FrameBuffer enabled, wait for complete video frames before playing them.
  • input_signal_output_mode: required(object)

    Output mode based on input signal events.

    • loss_of_input: required(one of freeze, black, blue, no_signal)

      Output mode based on loss of input event.

Example:

{
  "version": "1",
  "label": "SDI 1",
  "id": "b0d2da17-360a-4396-80a9-f620c4bb3885",
  "device_id": "a0e61a30-990b-11e5-8994-feff819cdc9f",
  "sdi_aud_chans_cfg": {
    "ch0": "a14f66a2-9910-11e5-8894-feff819cdc9f:0:1",
    "ch1": "a14f66a2-9910-11e5-8894-feff819cdc9f:1:1",
    "ch2": " :0:0",
    "ch3": " :0:0",
    "ch4": " :0:0",
    "ch5": " :0:0",
    "ch6": " :0:0",
    "ch7": " :0:0",
    "ch8": " :0:0",
    "ch9": " :0:0",
    "ch10": " :0:0",
    "ch11": " :0:0",
    "ch12": " :0:0",
    "ch13": " :0:0",
    "ch14": " :0:0",
    "ch15": " :0:0"
  },
  "line_offset": {
    "offset_mode": "1",
    "usec_offset": "207",
    "v_offset": "7",
    "h_offset": "0",
    "audio_delay": "64",
    "applied_audio_delay": "64",
    "status": "1",
    "frame_buffer": 0
  },
  "input_signal_output_mode": {
    "loss_of_input": "blue"
  }
}

  • sdiOutputId: (string - pattern: ^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-5][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$)

    Valid SDI Output identifier.

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

        • IP stream UUID.

        • Enable/Disable (1/0).
      • To unmap a SDI channel: " :0:0"
  • line_offset: required(object)

    Line offset configurations.

    • offset_mode: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} Line offset mode to use.

      • 0 = micro second offset mode.
      • 1 = line offset mode.
    • usec_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} uSecond to offset video from PTP when micro second offset mode is selected.

    • v_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} Vertical line offset when line offset mode is selected.

    • h_offset: required(string)

      {R/W} Horizontal pixel offset when line offset mode is selected.

    • audio_delay: required(string)

      {R/W} Audio delay to be applied. In step of 1/freq, where freq can be 48000 or 96000 (if supported by platform).

      • NOTE: Setting 0 will set automatic mode.
    • frame_buffer: required(one of 0, 1)

      {R/W} FrameBuffer enable switch.

      • 0 = FrameBuffer disabled, precise timing mode.
      • 1 = FrameBuffer enabled, wait for complete video frames before playing them.
  • input_signal_output_mode: required(object)

    Output mode based on input signal events.

    • loss_of_input: required(one of freeze, black, blue, no_signal)

      Output mode based on loss of input event.

  "sdi_aud_chans_cfg": {

    "ch2": " :0:0",
    "ch3": " :0:0",
    "ch4": "a34f66a2-9910-11e5-8894-feff819cdc9f:4:1",
    "ch5": " :0:0",
    "ch6": " :0:0",
    "ch7": "a24f66a2-9910-11e5-8894-feff819cdc9f:2:1",
    "ch8": " :0:0",
    "ch9": " :0:0",
    "ch10": " :0:0",
    "ch11": " :0:0",
    "ch12": " :0:0",
    "ch13": " :0:0",
    "ch14": " :0:0",
    "ch15": " :0:0"
  },
  "line_offset": {
    "offset_mode": "0",
    "usec_offset": "207",
    "v_offset": "15",
    "h_offset": "0",
    "audio_delay": "64",
    "frame_buffer": 0

    "loss_of_input": "blue"
  }
